the Commonwealth Games">Wrestling</a></li></ul>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p>The <b>Commonwealth Games</b>  are an international <a href="/wiki/Multi-sport_event" title="Multi-sport event">multi-sport event</a> involving athletes from the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Nations" title="Commonwealth of Nations">Commonwealth of Nations</a>. The event was first held in 1930, and has taken place every four years since then.<sup id="cite_ref-:1_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> The Commonwealth Games were known as the <b>British Empire Games</b> from 1930 to 1950, the <b>British Empire and Commonwealth Games</b> from 1954 to 1966, and <b>British Commonwealth Games</b> from 1970 to 1974. It is the world\'s first multi-sport event which inducted equal number of women\xe2\x80\x99s and men\xe2\x80\x99s medal events and was implemented recently in the 2018 Commonwealth Games.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Their creation was inspired by the  <a href="/wiki/Festival_of_the_Empire#Inter-Empire_Championships" class="mw-redirect" title="Festival of the Empire">Inter-Empire Championships</a>, as a part of the <a href="/wiki/Festival_of_Empire" title="Festival of Empire">Festival of Empire</a>, which were held in <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> in 1911. <a href="/wiki/Melville_Marks_Robinson" title="Melville Marks Robinson">Melville Marks Robinson</a> founded the games as the British Empire Games which were first hosted in <a href="/wiki/Hamilton,_Ontario" title="Hamilton, Ontario">Hamilton</a> in 1930.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> During the 20th and 21st centuries, the evolution of the games movement has resulted in several changes to the Commonwealth Games. Some of these adjustments include the creation of the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_Winter_Games" title="Commonwealth Winter Games">Commonwealth Winter Games</a> for snow and ice sports for the commonwealth athletes,<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_Paraplegic_Games" title="Commonwealth Paraplegic Games">Commonwealth Paraplegic Games</a> for commonwealth athletes with a disability<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> and the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_Youth_Games" title="Commonwealth Youth Games">Commonwealth Youth Games</a> for commonwealth athletes aged 14 to 18. The first edition of the winter games and paraplegic games were held in 1958 and <a href="/wiki/1962_Commonwealth_Paraplegic_Games" title="1962 Commonwealth Paraplegic Games">1962</a> respectively, with their last edition held in 1966 and <a href="/wiki/1974_Commonwealth_Paraplegic_Games" title="1974 Commonwealth Paraplegic Games">1974</a> respectively and the first youth games were held in <a href="/wiki/2000_Commonwealth_Youth_Games" title="2000 Commonwealth Youth Games">2000</a>. The 1942 and 1946 Commonwealth Games were cancelled because of the <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">second world war</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The Commonwealth Games are overseen by the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_Games_Federation" title="Commonwealth Games Federation">Commonwealth Games Federation</a> (CGF), which also controls the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_Games_sports" title="Commonwealth Games sports">sporting programme</a> and selects the host cities. The games movement consists of <a href="/wiki/List_of_international_sport_federations" class="mw-redirect" title="List of international sport federations">international sports federations</a> (IFs), <a href="/wiki/Category:Commonwealth_Games_Associations" title="Category:Commonwealth Games Associations">Commonwealth Games Associations</a> (CGAs), and organising committees for each specific Commonwealth Games. There are several rituals and symbols, such as the Commonwealth Games flag and <a href="/wiki/Queen%27s_Baton_Relay" title="Queen&#39;s Baton Relay">Queen\'s Baton</a>, as well as the opening and closing ceremonies. Over 5,000 athletes compete at the Commonwealth Games in more than 15 different sports and more than 250 events. The first, second, and third-place finishers in each event receive Commonwealth Games medals: gold, silver, and bronze, respectively. Apart from many <a href="/wiki/Olympic_sports" title="Olympic sports">Olympic sports</a>, the games also include some sports that are played predominantly in Commonwealth countries but which are not part of the Olympic programme, such as <a href="/wiki/Lawn_bowls" class="mw-redirect" title="Lawn bowls">lawn bowls</a>, <a href="/wiki/Netball" title="Netball">netball</a> and <a href="/wiki/Squash_(sport)" title="Squash (sport)">squash</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Although there are currently 53 members of the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Nations" title="Commonwealth of Nations">Commonwealth of Nations</a>, 71 teams currently participate in the Commonwealth Games, as a number of dependent territories compete under their own flags. The four <a href="/wiki/Home_Nations" title="Home Nations">Home Nations</a> of the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>\xe2\x80\x94<a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>, <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scotland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wales" title="Wales">Wales</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a>\xe2\x80\x94also send separate teams.\n</p><p>Nineteen cities in nine countries (counting England, Wales, and Scotland separately) have hosted the event. <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> has hosted the Commonwealth Games five times (<a href="/wiki/1938_Commonwealth_Games" class="mw-redirect" title="1938 Commonwealth Games">1938</a>, <a href="/wiki/1962_Commonwealth_Games" class="mw-redirect" title="1962 Commonwealth Games">1962</a>, <a href="/wiki/1982_Commonwealth_Games" title="1982 Commonwealth Games">1982</a>, <a href="/wiki/2006_Commonwealth_Games" title="2006 Commonwealth Games">2006</a> and <a href="/wiki/2018_Commonwealth_Games" title="2018 Commonwealth Games">2018</a>); this is more times than any other nation. Two cities have hosted Commonwealth Games more than once: <a href="/wiki/Auckland" title="Auckland">Auckland</a> (<a href="/wiki/1950_Commonwealth_Games" class="mw-redirect" title="1950 Commonwealth Games">1950</a>, <a href="/wiki/1990_Commonwealth_Games" title="1990 Commonwealth Games">1990</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Edinburgh" title="Edinburgh">Edinburgh</a> (<a href="/wiki/1970_Commonwealth_Games" class="mw-redirect" title="1970 Commonwealth Games">1970</a>, <a href="/wiki/1986_Commonwealth_Games" title="1986 Commonwealth Games">1986</a>).\n</p><p>Only six countries have attended every Commonwealth Games: <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>, <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a>, <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scotland</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Wales" title="Wales">Wales</a>. Australia has been the highest achieving team for twelve games, England for seven, and Canada for one.\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/2018_Commonwealth_Games" title="2018 Commonwealth Games">most recent Commonwealth Games</a> were held in <a href="/wiki/Gold_Coast,_Queensland" title="Gold Coast, Queensland">Gold Coast</a> from 4 to 15 April 2018. The <a href="/wiki/2022_Commonwealth_Games" title="2022 Commonwealth Games">next Commonwealth Games</a> are to be held in <a href="/wiki/Birmingham" title="Birmingham">Birmingham</a> from 27 July to 7 August 2022.\n</p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none" /><div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr"><h2>Contents</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>\n<ul>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-1"><a Games</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-5"><a href="#British_Empire_and_Commonwealth_Games"><span class="tocnumber">2.1.2</span> <span class="toctext">British Empire and Commonwealth class="tocnumber">3</span> <span class="toctext">Commonwealth Games Federation</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-14"><a href="#Queen&#39;s_Baton_Relay"><span class="tocnumber">4</span> <span class="toctext">Queen\'s Baton Relay</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-15"><a href="#Ceremonies"><span class="tocnumber">5</span> <span
